```html
<script>
  (function () {
    class BaseButtonComponent extends HTMLElement {
      constructor() {
        super();
        this.addEventListener('click', this.onClickButton.bind(this));
      }

      onClickButton(e) {
        const button = e.target.closest('.base-button');
        if (button) {
          const link = button.getAttribute('data-link');
          const target = button.getAttribute('data-target');
          if (link) {
            e.preventDefault();
            if (Shopify && Shopify.designMode) {
              if (link.includes('https://') || link.includes('http://')) {
                if (window.confirm(`This link cannot be opened inside the editor. It will be opened in a new window (${link})`)) {
                  return;
                } else {
                  return;
                }
              }
            }
            if (target == '_blank') {
              window.open(link, '_blank').focus();
            } else {
              window.location.href = link;
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (!customElements.get('base-button-component')) {
      customElements.define('base-button-component', BaseButtonComponent);
    }
  })();
</script>
```

```html
  <script>
     function initializeTabs() {
    const tabContainer = document.querySelector('.related-products-tabs');
    if (!tabContainer) return;

    const tabHeadings = tabContainer.querySelectorAll('.tab-heading');
    const tabContents = tabContainer.querySelectorAll('.tab-content');

    function showTab(index) {
      tabContents.forEach(content => {
        content.style.display = content.dataset.tabIndex === index ? 'block' : 'none';
      });
      tabHeadings.forEach(tab => {
        tab.classList.toggle('active', tab.dataset.tabIndex === index);
      });
    }

    tabHeadings.forEach(tab => {
      tab.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        showTab(this.dataset.tabIndex);
      });
    });

    showTab("0"); // Default to first tab
  }

  // Run on initial page load
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initializeTabs);

  // Re-run when section is re-rendered via theme editor
  document.addEventListener('shopify:section:load', function (event) {
    if (event.target.querySelector('.related-products-tabs')) {
      initializeTabs();
    }
  });
      
function initRecentlyViewedSlider(wrapper) {
  const grid = wrapper.querySelector('#recently-viewed-products .product-grid');
  const parent = wrapper.closest('.viewed-products');
  const prev = wrapper.querySelector('.viewed-products .prev');
  const next = wrapper.querySelector('.viewed-products .next');
  const progressFill = parent.querySelector('.fill-recen');
  const progressWrapper = parent.querySelector('.slider-progress');
  const totalCountEl = parent.querySelector('.slider-progress .re-toal');
  const currentIndexEl = parent.querySelector('.slider-progress .current-index');
  const gap = 20;
  let index = 0;

  if (!grid || !grid.children.length) return;

  const items = Array.from(grid.children);
  const totalItems = items.length;

  const getVisibleItems = () => {
    let container = grid;
    let containerWidth = container.clientWidth;
    let itemWidth = items[0]?.offsetWidth || 1;
    if (containerWidth==0) {
      const tabContent = container.closest('.tab-content');
      tabContent.style.display = 'block';
      containerWidth = container.clientWidth;
      itemWidth = items[0]?.offsetWidth || 1;
      tabContent.style.display = 'none';
    }
    return Math.max(1, Math.floor((containerWidth + 0) / (itemWidth + 0)));
  };

  const getTotalSteps = () => {
    const visibleItems = getVisibleItems();
    return Math.max(1, totalItems - visibleItems + 1);
  };

  let totalSteps = getTotalSteps();
  if (totalSteps == 1) {
    if (wrapper.querySelector('.slider-progress')) slider.querySelector('.slider-progress').style.display = 'none';
    if (prev) prev.remove();
    if (next) next.remove();
    return 0;
  }
  if (progressWrapper) progressWrapper.style.display = 'flex';
  if (totalSteps<2 && progressWrapper) progressWrapper.style.display = "none";

  const updateProgress = () => {
    if (progressFill) {
      const percent = totalSteps <= 1 ? 100 : (index / (totalSteps - 1)) * 100;
      progressFill.style.width = `${Math.min(percent, 100)}%`;
    }
    //console.log(totalCountEl);
    if (currentIndexEl) currentIndexEl.textContent = String(index + 1).padStart(2, '0');
    if (totalCountEl) totalCountEl.textContent = String(totalSteps).padStart(2, '0');
  };

  const updateButtons = () => {
    prev.disabled = index <= 0;
    next.disabled = index >= totalSteps - 1;
  };

  const move = (dir) => {
    totalSteps = getTotalSteps(); // Recalculate on resize or move
    if (dir === 'next') {
      index = Math.min(index + 1, totalSteps - 1);
    } else {
      index = Math.max(index - 1, 0);
    }

    const targetItem = items[index];
    grid.scrollTo({ left: targetItem.offsetLeft, behavior: 'smooth' });

    updateProgress();
    updateButtons();
  };

  prev?.addEventListener('click', () => move('prev'));
  next?.addEventListener('click', () => move('next'));

  // Manual scroll detect
  let scrollTimeout;
  grid.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
    clearTimeout(scrollTimeout);
    scrollTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      const scrollLeft = grid.scrollLeft;
      let closestIndex = 0;
      let minDist = Infinity;

      items.forEach((item, i) => {
        const dist = Math.abs(item.offsetLeft - scrollLeft);
        if (dist < minDist) {
          minDist = dist;
          closestIndex = i;
        }
      });

      index = Math.min(closestIndex, getTotalSteps() - 1);
      updateProgress();
      updateButtons();
    }, 100);
  });

  updateProgress();
  updateButtons();
}



</script>

  

  
      <script>
        async function loadRecentlyViewed() {
        const container = document.getElementById('recently-viewed-products');
        if (!container) return;
    
        const grid = container.querySelector('.product-grid');
        if (!grid) return;
    
        const rawHandles = localStorage.getItem('recently_viewed');
        const handles = JSON.parse(rawHandles || '[]');
        const currentHandle = 'gift-card';
        const maxProducts = 12;
        const filtered = handles.filter(h => h !== currentHandle).slice(0, maxProducts);
    
        const progressElement = container.querySelector('.slider-progress');
        const tabContents = container.closest('.tab-content');
        const tabIndex = tabContents.dataset.tabIndex;
        if (!filtered.length) {
          console.info('No recently viewed items to show.');
          if (progressElement) progressElement.style.display = 'none';
          if (tabContents) tabContents.style.display = 'none';
          const relatedTabs = tabContents.closest('.related-products-tabs');
          const heading = relatedTabs.querySelector(`.tab-heading[data-tab-index="${tabIndex}"]`);
          if (heading) heading.style.display = 'none';
          if (tabIndex==0) {
            const tabContainer = document.querySelector('.related-products-tabs');
            if (!tabContainer) return;
            const tabHeadings = tabContainer.querySelectorAll('.tab-heading');
            const tabContents = tabContainer.querySelectorAll('.tab-content');
            function showTab(index) {
              tabContents.forEach(content => {
                content.style.display = content.dataset.tabIndex === index ? 'block' : 'none';
              });
              tabHeadings.forEach(tab => {
                tab.classList.toggle('active', tab.dataset.tabIndex === index);
              });
            }
            showTab("1");
          }
          return;
        }

        const queryParams = new URLSearchParams({
          section_id: 'recently-viewed-product-render',
          media_size: 'portrait',
        });
        const mediaSize = queryParams.get('media_size'); // Get the value from URLSearchParams
          
        const fetchProduct = async (handle) => {
          try {
            const res = await fetch(`/products/${handle}?${queryParams}`);
            const html = await res.text();
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.innerHTML = html;
            const li = div.querySelector('li.grid__item');
            if (!li) console.warn(`No product card found in response for ${handle}`);
            return li;
          } catch (e) {
            console.warn(`Failed to load product: ${handle}`, e);
            return null;
          }
        };
    
        const products = await Promise.all(filtered.map(fetchProduct));
        const validProducts = products.filter(Boolean);
        if (!validProducts.length) return;
    
        grid.innerHTML = ''; // Clear old content
        grid.setAttribute('data-slides', filtered.length);
        grid.classList.add(`product-grid-${filtered.length}`);;
        validProducts.forEach(el => grid.appendChild(el));
        container.hidden = false;
        validProducts.forEach(el => {
          grid.appendChild(el);
          const slideshow = el.querySelector('.product-images-slideshow');
          if (slideshow && mediaSize) {
            slideshow.classList.add(`media--${mediaSize}`);
          }
        });
        if (typeof initRecentlyViewedSlider === 'function') {
          initRecentlyViewedSlider(container);
        }
      }
    
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', loadRecentlyViewed);
    
      document.addEventListener('shopify:section:load', (event) => {
        if (event.target.querySelector('#recently-viewed-products')) {
          loadRecentlyViewed();
        }
      });
      </script>
  
  
</div>

<script>
  class ProductRecommendations extends HTMLElement {
  observer = undefined;

  constructor() {
    super();
  }

  connectedCallback() {
    this.initializeRecommendations(this.dataset.productId);
  }

  initializeRecommendations(productId) {
    this.observer?.unobserve(this);
    this.observer = new IntersectionObserver(
      (entries, observer) => {
        if (!entries[0].isIntersecting) return;
        observer.unobserve(this);
        this.loadRecommendations(productId);
      },
      { rootMargin: '0px 0px 400px 0px' }
    );
    this.observer.observe(this);
  }

  loadRecommendations(productId) {
    fetch(`${this.dataset.url}&product_id=${productId}&section_id=${this.dataset.sectionId}`)
      .then((response) => response.text())
      .then((text) => {
        const html = document.createElement('div');
        html.innerHTML = text;
        const recommendations = html.querySelector('product-recommendations');

        if (recommendations?.innerHTML.trim().length) {
          this.innerHTML = recommendations.innerHTML;
          this.initSlider(); // Initialize the slider after loading recommendations
          this.initSliders();
        }

        if (!this.querySelector('slideshow-component') && this.classList.contains('complementary-products')) {
          this.remove();
        }

        if (html.querySelector('.grid__item')) {
          this.classList.add('product-recommendations--loaded');
        }
      })
      .catch((e) => {
        console.error(e);
      });
  }

  
initSliders() {
  const slider = document.querySelector('.complementary-slider');
  if (!slider) return;

  const items = [...slider.querySelectorAll('.slider__slide')];
  const itemCount = items.length;

  const prevBtn = document.querySelector('.slider-button--prev');
  const nextBtn = document.querySelector('.slider-button--next');

  let currentIndex = 0;

  const updateButtons = () => {
    // Nếu muốn disable button thì mở comment
    // prevBtn.disabled = currentIndex === 0;
    // nextBtn.disabled = currentIndex >= itemCount - 1;
  };

  const scrollToIndex = (index) => {
    const target = items[index];
    if (!target) return;

    const scrollLeft =
      slider.scrollLeft + (target.offsetLeft - slider.offsetLeft);

    slider.scrollTo({ left: scrollLeft, behavior: 'smooth' });

    currentIndex = index;
    updateButtons();
  };

  nextBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (currentIndex < itemCount - 1) scrollToIndex(currentIndex + 1);
  });

  prevBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (currentIndex > 0) scrollToIndex(currentIndex - 1);
  });

  let resizeTimer;
  let lastIsWide = window.innerWidth > 750;

  window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
    clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
    resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      const isWide = window.innerWidth > 750;
      if (isWide !== lastIsWide) {
        this.initSlider?.();
        this.initSliders?.();
        lastIsWide = isWide;
      }
    }, 200);
  });

  // Init trạng thái ban đầu
  updateButtons();
}

initSlider() {
  const container = document.querySelector('product-recommendations .product-slider .product-grid');
  if (!container) return;

  const items = Array.from(container.children);
  const totalItems = items.length;

  const prevButton = document.querySelector('product-recommendations .product-slider .slider-button.prev');
  const nextButton = document.querySelector('product-recommendations .product-slider .slider-button.next');
  const progressWrapper = document.querySelector('product-recommendations .slider-progress');
  const progressFill = progressWrapper?.querySelector('.progress-fill');
  const currentIndexEl = progressWrapper?.querySelector('.current-index');
  const totalCountEl = progressWrapper?.querySelector('.total-count');

  // === Calculate visible slides based on container width ===
  const getVisibleSlides = () => {
    let containerWidth = container.clientWidth;
    let itemWidth = items[0]?.offsetWidth || 1;
    if (containerWidth==0) {
      const tabContent = container.closest('.tab-content');
      tabContent.style.display = 'block';
      containerWidth = container.clientWidth;
      itemWidth = items[0]?.offsetWidth || 1;
      tabContent.style.display = 'none';
    }
    const style = getComputedStyle(container);
    const gap = parseInt(style.columnGap || style.gap || 0);
    return Math.max(1, Math.floor((containerWidth + 0) / (itemWidth + 0)));
  };

  const visibleSlides = getVisibleSlides();
  const totalSteps = Math.max(1, totalItems - visibleSlides + 1);
  if (progressWrapper) progressWrapper.style.display = 'flex';
  if (totalSteps == 1) {
    if (progressWrapper) progressWrapper.style.display = 'none';
    if (prevButton) prevButton.remove();
    if (nextButton) nextButton.remove();
    return 0;
  }
  if (totalCountEl) totalCountEl.textContent = String(totalSteps).padStart(2, '0');

  let currentIndex = 0;

  const scrollToIndex = (index) => {
    index = Math.max(0, Math.min(index, totalSteps - 1));
    const target = items[index];
    if (!target) return;

    container.scrollTo({
      left: target.offsetLeft,
      behavior: 'smooth'
    });

    currentIndex = index;
    updateUI();
  };

  const updateUI = () => {
    const step = currentIndex + 1;

    if (currentIndexEl) currentIndexEl.textContent = String(step).padStart(2, '0');

    if (progressFill && totalSteps > 1) {
      const percent = ((step - 1) / (totalSteps - 1)) * 100;
      progressFill.style.width = `${percent}%`;
    }

    prevButton?.classList.toggle('disabled', currentIndex === 0);
    nextButton?.classList.toggle('disabled', currentIndex >= totalSteps - 1);
  };

  prevButton?.addEventListener('click', () => scrollToIndex(currentIndex - 1));
  nextButton?.addEventListener('click', () => scrollToIndex(currentIndex + 1));

  // Auto update index on scroll
  let scrollTimer;
  container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
    clearTimeout(scrollTimer);
    scrollTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      const scrollLeft = container.scrollLeft;

      let closestIndex = 0;
      let minDistance = Infinity;

      for (let i = 0; i < totalSteps; i++) {
        const dist = Math.abs(items[i].offsetLeft - scrollLeft);
        if (dist < minDistance) {
          minDistance = dist;
          closestIndex = i;
        }
      }

      if (closestIndex !== currentIndex) {
        currentIndex = closestIndex;
        updateUI();
      }
    }, 100);
  });

  updateUI();
}

}

customElements.define('product-recommendations', ProductRecommendations);
</script>



</section>
```
